  * grade_story_10.txt (grade=5.8)
    The story demonstrates creativity in merging science fiction elements with the intimate act of baking as emotional healing. The central metaphor shows promise, and the atmospheric elements effectively support the character's journey. However, the narrative suffers from excessive abstraction and limited specificity about the character's past actions, relationships, and concrete stakes. The writing style, while occasionally evocative, tends toward generic emotional descriptors rather than unique insights.
